[CrestParamSet MyCRESTPAR]
wm_grid=parameters/crest_Wm.tif
b_grid=parameters/crest_b.tif

ke=1.0
fc=1.00
iwu=0.0

[kwparamset MyKWPAR]
alpha_grid=parameters/kw_alpha.tif
beta_grid=parameters/kw_beta.tif

under_grid=parameters/crest_Fc_Ksat.tif

alpha=1.0

beta=1.0

th=12.0
isu=0.0

MODEL=crest
ROUTING=KW
BASIN=0

ROUTING_PARAM_Set=MyKWPAR
TIMESTEP=30u
TIME_BEGIN={TIMEBEGIN}
TIME_WARMEND={TIMEWARMEND}
TIME_STATE={TIMESTATE}
TIME_END={TIMEEND}
